Autopsy of a Female Corpse on the Bund

At 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, a female corpse was discovered on the Bund behind the Ruirong Shipyard in Yangshupu. After investigation by various police stations, the case was reported to the Huishan police station, which dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. The corpse was then taken to the Feilun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, the case was reported to the Provisional Court, which appointed Judge Sun Yuan to conduct an autopsy. According to the complaint filed by Bellinger, the Western detective chief of the Huishan police station, he went to investigate after receiving the report yesterday afternoon and found that the deceased was female, about ten years old. There were finger marks on her nostrils and rope marks on her neck. Her mouth was stuffed with cotton wool. However, her family has not yet been found. Judge Sun asked if there were any yarn factories nearby and whether they had been investigated. The Western detective chief replied that he had not had time to do so yesterday but would investigate in detail today. Since the deceased had no family, Judge Sun ordered the Pushan Benevolent Hall to provide a coffin and burial, and instructed the police to investigate the truth of the matter for further investigation.

Assault During a Gambling Dispute

In a small teahouse in Qichangzhai, Pudong, at 10:00 PM the night before last, several customers were gathered to play Pai Gow. The bankers were two brothers, Zou Weijin and Zou Weiyin, from Huai'an. Suddenly, a gambler named Sha Jinbiao from Qingjiang accused the banker Weiyin of cheating by using sleight of hand, causing him to lose six yuan. He demanded the money back, and an argument ensued, leading to a fight. Sha then grabbed two iron rods and attacked the Zou brothers, injuring Weiyin on the head. Patrolmen from the Third District police station arrived and took Sha, along with the iron rods, and the Zou brothers to the Third District police station. Sha claimed that he had been cheated, while the Zou brothers claimed that Sha had tried to borrow money and, when refused, intentionally caused trouble. After reviewing the statements, the district chief ordered the police to send the defendants and the weapons to the District Court for investigation yesterday.

The Intentions of Accountants and Apprentices Are Truly Unfathomable

▲ Conspiring to Steal Silver from the Shop Owner

▲ And Then Committing Arson

On the morning of January 30th of this year, the Tongfengxing Foreign Goods Company, located at No. 63 Huolun Mill Street in the French Concession, owned by Xu Zenggui, was set on fire by the accountant Qian Yunfeng in collusion with the apprentice Fu Heqing. They also stole 7,400 yuan in cash. Detective Mao Jinsheng of the French police learned of this and arrested Fu Heqing, who confessed that Qian Yunfeng was hiding in Xiangshan Road, Zhabei. Mao went there and arrested Qian, taking him back to the French police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the French court for investigation. First, Xu Zenggui, the owner of Tongfengxing, reported the arson and theft, stating that the company had lost a total of 11,189 yuan in cash.

After recovering 7,400 yuan, there is still a shortage of 3,789 yuan. He requested an investigation. Fu Heqing confessed that he was 19 years old and had been an apprentice in the plaintiff's shop for two years. Qian Yunfeng joined the shop as an accountant last year and became friends with him. Not long after, Qian used a false account to take 300 yuan. After it was discovered, his relatives mediated. Soon after, he secretly committed fraud, which was discovered by the shop owner and was being investigated. Qian Yunfeng asked him to go out and play, saying that the shop owner was bad and they should find a way to harm him. He told him where the shop owner kept the silver and gave him a key to steal it. The first time, he stole 1,000 yuan, the second time 2,500 yuan, and the third time 3,900 yuan, for a total of 7,400 yuan. He sent the money to his cousin Fu Heming on Baille Road. On the morning of the 30th of last month, he met Qian at the corner of Mill Street, who gave him a bottle of kerosene and told him to pour it on the cotton quilt in the shop and set it on fire to cover up the crime. Unexpectedly, the plot was discovered and he was arrested. He asked for leniency. Qian Yunfeng confessed to instigating the theft of silver and arson. The rest of his testimony was the same as Fu's. Fu Heming testified that Fu Heqing was his cousin. When he brought the large sum of money to deposit it, he said he had won it at the Gold Exchange. He was deceived for a while and believed it was true. Not long after, he took away 5,000 yuan. Later, the merchant saw that his behavior was suspicious and went to the shop to investigate, only to find out that it was stolen. He then returned the remaining money to the shop owner. After reviewing the statements, the Chinese and Western officials sentenced Fu and Qian to five years each in the Western prison as a warning, and sent them to the inland court for trial.

Kidnapping a Woman and Detaining Her for Two Months

Gu Qungan, the 16-year-old daughter of Gu Yichun, a native of Jiangbei who lives in Shudeli, Pingjili Road in the French Concession, was kidnapped by Jiang Xiaoyuanzi, who lives on Lafayette Road, to Wuxi on December 17th of last year. The girl's father discovered this and reported it to the French police, who ordered Detective Ding Wensheng to arrest Jiang and the girl and bring them back to the French police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the French court for investigation. The plaintiff, Gu Yichun, stated that his daughter had been kidnapped twice. The first time, he did not pursue the matter because it concerned his reputation. Unexpectedly, she was kidnapped again this time, so he reported it to the police for arrest. Jiang Xiaoyuanzi, who has been married for only a short time, dared to kidnap a girl, which is extremely illegal. He requested a severe sentence. Gu Qungan testified that she had known Jiang for two years and that she had voluntarily run away with Jiang to Wuxi and was not kidnapped by him. Jiang Xiaoyuanzi's testimony was the same. Judge Zhu sentenced Jiang Xiaoyuanzi to two months in the Western prison as a warning and ordered Gu's daughter to be taken back by her father for discipline.

The Efficacy of New Medicine for Lung Disease and Hemoptysis

The Popularity of Taiziling Light Bulbs

In recent years, the domestic electric light industry has become increasingly developed, sufficient for imported light bulbs, which increase every year. The most famous one on the market today is the Taiziling brand, produced by a famous Hungarian factory. The filament of this light bulb is coiled into a screw shape, which is elastic. Even if it is shaken, it will not be damaged. Most of the damage to light bulbs is caused by the breaking of the filament. Taiziling light bulbs are not only durable but also have brighter light and save more electricity than other light bulbs. They are also priced very cheaply, so after being shipped to Shanghai, they are sold very widely. It is said that in the past two months, more than 200,000 bulbs have been sold, which shows their value. It is also said that the electrical material stores that sell Taiziling light bulbs say that Taiziling light bulbs are praised by people and can increase the credibility of the dealers. Therefore, all major electrical material stores in this city sell Taiziling light bulbs. The ones with the largest sales are Fulai, Hongkang, Huitong, Xiefeng, Tianfa, and Yongda, etc. The general manager is Xinchang Company at No. 15 Museum Road.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory issued a weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday, stating that the weather along the coast of Shandong is clear and cold, there are clouds in the Yangtze River basin, the weather in the south is cloudy, and there is rainfall in coastal areas. The coasts of the country all have winds from the northwest to northeast, as is appropriate for the season. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 39.9 degrees and the lowest was 27.3 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 43.3 degrees and the lowest was 20.3 degrees.

Free Talk

Dismissed with a Laugh

— Sea Guest

A: Your wife has been ill for a long time. Is she fully recovered now?

B: Although she has fully recovered, she is very weak and cannot handle some household chores. But yesterday she went out for a long time and bought a lot of things back.

A: According to that beggar, this hospital was entirely funded by him. Is that true? B: Hmph, because of his improper behavior, he was driven out by his father and used the share of the property that should have been given to him to build this hospital.

Writer: This is my masterpiece. Do you find it satisfactory after reading it?

Friend: How could it not be? I only read one page, and I was so satisfied that I didn't want to read the second page.

A: I met an old friend in the street, which made me think of you.

B: Thank you, thank you. But what's the matter?

A: He once borrowed 100 yuan from me, and the principal and interest are still nowhere to be found.

Tooth Patient: This set of dentures you made for me is too big.

Dentist: Please sit down. Let me enlarge your mouth a little.

A Record of the Gold Panners at the Foot of Jinping Mountain

— Old Slave

Recorded in February of the seventh year of the Republic, serving in the Jialing military. The mountains and rivers are beautiful, and the people are elegant. Even amidst the turmoil of war, conversations are refined and romantic. Du Shaoling's "Stone Cabinet Poem" and Wu Daozi's "Jialing River" poem contain books. What else is needed? A guest mentioned the beauty of Jinping Mountain, with double citrus and wine, to listen to the sound of the orioles, and hundreds of trees with mixed flowers, to happily watch the dance of the warblers. This place is quite poetic. Who would have thought that the foot of the mountain would be the dwelling place of gold? Approaching the stream to find a crossing, perhaps returning to Deer Gate. Breaking bamboo to search for sand, this is what is called panning. Thousands of families gather, rotating every fifty days. Although the amount taken is not much, the principle is in order. The Jialing River produces gold, and panning began in the Tang Dynasty. One or two days, without gaining a handful of fullness. Thousands and millions, will there be a distinction between righteousness and profit? When the sun first rises, the bugle sounds loudly. Once gathered, there is a natural order. Then they raise their bamboo tools. Gains and losses are not allowed to be disputed. Watching the time of casting the net, all forces rise together. Carrying and going away, hammering and forging are diligent. Sand and stone turn into flying dust, and pure gold comes out. The gains in ten days do not exceed a fraction of a millimeter. Accumulating over time, it reaches millions. As for the blessings bestowed by heaven, people are accustomed to labor. Arriving every ten days, lifting the net will surely yield. Not fearing the cold or heat, why worry about the wind and rain? Passing it on to children and grandchildren, without asking for help from other mountains. This is the wealthy gold panner. There are also those who are not blessed by heaven, and their fate is not as good as others. The former returns fully loaded, while the latter returns despondently. Although the river flow is fixed, meeting is without fate. It is evident that the furnace fire is in vain, and it is mostly related to a poor fate. This is the poor gold panner. Therefore, observing the wealth and poverty of gold panners, wealth and status are in heaven. The ancient saying is clear, and this is even more credible.

Now, the price of gold is soaring, and the value of silver has fallen sharply. To save the country, there must be a plan to increase revenue. Why envy the fish while standing by the pond? It is better to cast a net to gain something real. Why not solidify the prison after a sheep is lost? Moreover, the United States is rich in gold, and Japan's gold has been deregulated. Although our country is a silver-using country, wealth is hidden in the mountains, and it may not produce gold. The gold of Mohe is already produced in huge quantities every year, and the production of the Jinsha River is even more endless. If there is a way to promote it and store it properly, why worry about the preciousness of gold and being taken advantage of by other countries? If you say that digging a well when thirsty will eventually lead to water, and drawing cakes to satisfy hunger will cure the disease in the stomach. I heard that the nugget gold of the three northeastern provinces has been seized and privatized by warlords. I have seen that the more than a thousand households of gold panners in the Jialing River have been robbed and completely taken away by mountain bandits. Therefore, what China is facing today is not the gold of international trade becoming more and more expensive, but the lack of protection by the government in the gold-producing areas within the country. Peach blossoms overflow on the river, but the hall of refusing gold still exists. Why is the gold in the gold pit not mined? (Taohua Pass belongs to Lishui County, Zhejiang) In the midst of the Phoebe zhennan enclosure, does the treasure trove still exist? Why is the gold in the gold mine not taken? (Nanmuwei belongs to Badong County, Hubei) In addition, such as Nanmeng and Beimeng in Yunnan, and Wanshi Ping in Sichuan, and Dongqilusi in Xinjiang, all are gold-producing areas. It is a pity that they are abandoned and not taken. Because of the record of gold panning in the Jialing River, it is attached to the notes. Moreover, international trade requires gold as a standard of parity. How can China, which stands in the world, not change to the gold standard? The Ministry of Finance once had a proposal for a nominal gold standard of thirty-eight taels. Tang Mingshui also had regulations for gold coins. Now, in view of the urgency of the market and the fierceness of the commercial war, the implementation of the gold standard cannot be delayed. The mining and protection of gold mines cannot be delayed. If you believe in my words, you must know more about it to promote its realization.

New Talk in the Capital

— Chunhua

The new building of the Ministry of Railways is 50% complete. It is purely in the style of a palace. The roof is painted in various shades of blue. It is roughly the same as the Examination Yuan. However, the Examination Yuan was transformed from the Temple of the Martial God and is still constrained by the old appearance. It is not as fresh and new as the Ministry of Railways. The stone lions in front of the gate have been transported and displayed.

Zhongshan Road starts outside Haining Gate and leads directly to the mausoleum of the Premier, stretching more than twenty li. The project cannot be said to be anything but vast. However, because it was built hastily to complete it before the transfer of the remains, there are several places where asphalt was laid that are not very effective. For example, a section in front of the Ministry of the Navy.

Many potholes have been found. The people of Beijing jokingly call it "road sores".

Recently, the fad of pure singing has become popular in Beijing. The so-called pure singing involves a group of several female singers who sell their songs in tea houses around the Confucius Temple. This is what the Southerners call flower tea houses. It originally only existed in the Confucius Temple. Recently, several houses have been found in Jixiang Street in the north of the city. This is not because Beijing people are truly fond of opera, but because there are no other better forms of entertainment to replace it.

During the Lunar New Year, the various commercial markets in Beijing still entered a state of celebrating the New Year. Most businesses still closed for five days. Because it was rumored a few days ago that the police bureau was strictly enforcing the law, such as those who changed the couplets on the door or those who made a bow on the street to say congratulations, would each be fined five gold coins. As a result, there were about three or four tenths fewer households changing Spring Couplets in the streets and alleys than in the past. Those who celebrated the New Year on the street were even less numerous.

A Record of Weng Zhong Crying at Night

— Zheng Yimei

Weng Zhong is a stone statue in the cemetery. There is no spirituality or emotion to speak of. But now it is heard crying. This is also strange. At the foot of Zhixing Mountain in Wu County, there is Jin Suwu, where dozens of families live, making a living by farming, plowing, gathering firewood, and chopping wood. They are simple and have an ancient atmosphere. To the east of the fields, there is the tomb of a certain great official. The construction is extremely grand. However, the descendants are very few. Over the years, no one has swept or visited it. Brambles and thorns are rampant. Weng Zhong is broken. Only one remains. He still stands in the setting sun, like the Spirit Light of Lu. One night, a certain villager, Jia, returned from gambling at night. The north wind howled. The cold air cut to the bone. Jia shrank uncontrollably. When he came to the side of the tomb, he suddenly heard _ chu xu ying, like crying or whistling. The sound came from Weng Zhong. Jia was shocked. He returned home and fell ill for several days. Therefore, it spread far and wide, saying that Weng Zhong was causing trouble, crying at night to haunt people. Some burned incense and kowtowed to seek to avoid disaster. Some proposed to destroy Weng Zhong to eliminate evil spirits. Different opinions were seen and could not be decided. Finally, a certain Yi, who was known for his courage, led the crowd to destroy it. But Weng Zhong had already fallen to the grass, and the night crying was still the same. Yi took advantage of the bright moonlight to investigate the difference. He finally realized that the so-called night cry was the sound of the owl screeching in the tomb tree. The nest was destroyed, and the owl left. The crying sound stopped from then on. This matter is similar to the incident of the god in a certain ancient temple in Jiading during the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty. The temple had been without incense for a long time. The roof was about to collapse. A certain student, because he was scolded by his teacher, went out in a huff at night and stayed in the ancient temple. However, he could not sleep, tossing and turning. Suddenly, he heard the sound of moving and moving. In the faint moonlight, he saw the sleeves of the robe of the god in the niche moving without wind. He ran away in fright, panting and sweating. People asked for the details. Therefore, the spirit of the temple god was rumored. It was greatly decorated. When the god's robe was changed, the mice scurried. The mice were nesting in the sleeves of the robe. This sound of moving and moving and moving without wind was caused by this. The ancients said, "Evil arises from people." Seeing this, it is even more credible.

Random Gleanings from a Spring Banquet

— Pei Jiu

The Lion Grove in Wuzhong was created by the recluse Ni Yunlin. It is secluded and winding, possessing the wonders of forests, valleys, streams, and gorges. It has long been a scenic spot in Wuzhong. After being acquired by a certain person and undergoing major renovations, it is like a mountain forest wild man suddenly donning splendid robes, losing its original open and unrestrained charm. Discerning people all lament this. On the eve of the Beginning of Spring, Yao Zifen wined me at his residence. Zifen is fond of books and paintings, and his four walls are hung with works by famous contemporary artists, a dazzling array, a feast for the eyes. Among them is a vertical scroll of a corner of the Lion Grove, copied by Fan Shaoyun in the style of Ni Yunlin. Viewing it, one's poetic thoughts well up, unconsciously giving rise to a nostalgic feeling for the past. On the left of the painting is a strange peak, its shape resembling a crouching lion with its head raised and roaring. The piled-up stones show no trace of artificiality. Slightly to the right are several clumps of tall bamboos and a simple cottage, interspersed with various trees. The scenery is pure, sparse, and utterly free from mundane concerns, seeming not to be a place for humans. According to this painting, it must have been a meticulously structured work from a real-life sketch by Ni Yunlin himself. Moreover, Shaoyun's brushwork is also cautious and attentive, so it is sufficient to resemble the original. Now that the face of the Lion Grove is completely changed, this painting, although not a complete portrayal, can serve as a "Han Guan Yi Guan" (a model to learn about old traditions). I heard that this painting by Shaoyun was once exhibited at a certain "Leng Hong Exhibition." Many were fond of it, but it was eventually acquired by Zifen, which is indeed something to congratulate Zifen on. However, I also heard that Shaoyun had another painting at the time, also a copy of a corner of the Lion Grove, and it could have been paired with this one, but Zifen did not acquire it. I cannot help but feel sorry for Zifen.

The next evening, I dined at the residence of Wu Zidi Gang. I met Shaoyun at the gathering. During the meal, we played finger-guessing games and passed around wine cups, accompanied by Kunqu opera, enjoying the pleasure of friends at a gathering. Shaoyun, flushed with wine and in high spirits, wielded his brush and created a vertical scroll of bamboo and rocks, imitating Zhao Mengfu of the Yuan dynasty, quite like him. After the painting was completed, Di Gang asked You Xuanfu to inscribe a poem on it to commemorate this moment. Xuanfu immediately composed a quatrain: "Strange rocks, jagged, threatening to fly, / Tall bamboos, sheltering, leaning close by. / Knowing it's hard to please the eyes of the day, / I'll buy a green mountain, plant ferns, and fatten myself." Xuanfu had previously been a writer of popular fiction and was well-known in the storytelling world for many years. Now, reading his poem, it seems to express a sense of being out of step with the times. As the wine was about to run out, Xuanfu showed us a painting by Cheng Shaochuan, "Red Trees and Green Mountains, Good for a Boat Ride." The brushwork was modeled after Tang Yin. It was said to be a farewell gift for Xuanfu's trip to his family home in Zhejiang. Shaochuan is Shaoyun's indoor disciple. He is upright and unconventional, drifting under the Suzhou Terrace, quite frustrated. Now, reading his painting, his skill has reached perfection. Surely he will surpass his teacher. Poetry must be perfected through hardship. Is it also true that painting must be perfected through hardship?

The Water-Ice Beggar

— Xu Xiaoting

For the past month, the weather in Jiangbei has been extraordinarily cold. When we sleep on our beds, it is no different from lying on the ice-skating rink in Beiping's Sanhai Park. Sometimes, when I hold a pen to write, the pen is as cold as iron, much like an autumn insect clinging to a tree, without any warmth. One day, I happened to go to the South Park in the town to sip tea. On the way, I saw a beggar carrying a bamboo basket. The basket was full of ice cubes. The beggar took out the ice and ate it, chewing with a sound. In less than half an hour, he had eaten it all. He went along the road begging for money, his attitude calm and unhurried, without any hesitation. Those who saw it were amazed. A young man asked him, "Do you feel cold eating ice?" The beggar said, "The ice breaks as soon as it enters my mouth, and melts as I chew it. How can it be cold?" The young man said, "I will give you thirty catties of ice. If you can eat it all, I will give you ten small silver dollars." The beggar agreed readily. The young man then knocked off many pieces of ice from the stream, resembling thick sheets of glass, and weighed them to the required amount, giving them to the beggar to eat. The beggar ate it without any difficulty. The crisp and clear sound of chewing ice was astonishing to hear. The young man, amazed and surprised, gave him the silver dollars. By noon, the ice was gone. The beggar then left leisurely. At that time, the weather was very cold. We were warming ourselves around the stove, yet we still felt the cold invading us. The beggar, however, was lightly clothed and ate ice with relish. It is truly an extraordinary thing.

Snippets of Common Knowledge

— Tang Binhua

When taking the train, you can sit in second class with a third-class ticket, as long as you order several large dishes and tip the attendant to find a comfortable seat. The attendant will then lead you to second class. Even if the tickets are checked, the attendant will surely give a heads-up.

When entering a hotel, without waiting for the room attendant to speak, first ask him for paper and a pen and write down your name and occupation. The room attendant will know you are an experienced customer and will definitely not overcharge you.

When going to a dim sum shop to eat noodles, tell the waiter that you want lean meat in your meat noodles and the original flavor in your fish noodles. The waiter will not dare to be negligent, and the noodles you eat will be more authentic than others.

When taking a rickshaw and you don't know the way, don't bargain. When you arrive at your destination, just find a policeman and ask him how much it should cost from where you came. You will definitely not be cheated, and the rickshaw driver will not say a word.

Warmth in the Heart (126)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 8: A Delicate Bird Sings Among the Festive Banners, A Good Bird Chooses a Tree When the Golden House is Adorned

Shi Chen said, "Although I'm not from Nanjing, I lived there for a long time. You say you seem to have seen me before, and I also seem to have seen you. Let me ask you, where did you live near Hanxi Gate?" Ruiyun said, "At first, we lived in a place called Shuangshigu (Double Stone Drum). I often asked my mother what Shuangshigu meant. She said there used to be two stone drum steps there, but we couldn't find any stone drums. Later, my father couldn't find work and was very poor, so we borrowed a few small houses behind the Zhang family's garden. We lived there until the Zhang family sold the garden." Shi Chen couldn't help but clap his hands and said, "That's right, that's right! What a coincidence! At that time, Ruiyun was startled by Zuo Shichen and said, "Second Young Master, what are you doing? You scared me!" Shichen hugged her again and said, "Don't be afraid. I really did see you in Nanjing. Isn't the Zhang family you're talking about Zhang Huantong's family?" Ruiyun shook her head and said, "I don't know about that. The owner was still young. We called him Master Zhang. He was very kind. I've been to his wife's room upstairs a few times. She was very affectionate with me. Whenever I went, she would always give me a lot of things and often asked me to go there to play. Now they've sold the house and I don't know where they've gone." Zuo Shichen said, "Let me tell you, that Master Zhang is a friend of mine. He came to Shanghai a couple of years ago. Now some people say he's gone to Hubei. His wife naturally went with him. I remember five or six years ago, I was living in Nanjing, and a friend wanted to see Master Zhang's house, so we went to his back garden. Weren't you living at the back entrance of their garden? The garden was very desolate. There was a little girl, about eight or nine years old, barefoot and disheveled, following us, running around. Now that I think about it, it must have been you!" Ruiyun said, "Nonsense! There are many little girls in Nanjing. How do you know it was me?" Shichen said, "It's definitely you. Who else lived at the back entrance of the Zhang family's garden?" Ruiyun was moved by his words and seemed to have seen Shichen before, but after five or six years, who could remember? She just felt that he looked somewhat familiar. She then said, "There are many sisters in my family. How can you be sure it was me?" Shichen said, "Ah, I remember! That day, Master Zhang even called you Second Miss. Are you the second child in your family?" After hearing him say that, Ruiyun thought, "Could it really be him who saw me? What a coincidence that we met again here?" She then said, "Second Young Master, don't tell anyone that I'm from Nanjing. My mother only allows me to say that I'm from Suzhou, that she gave birth to me and raised me. She says that to all the guests. Otherwise, she will scold me." Shichen said, "Do they often scold you here?" Ruiyun said, "It's okay."

Also, Osaka spot yarn report: 20-count Blue Fish, 173 yuan, up 3 yuan, equivalent to Shanghai standard 178 taels and 6 mace; 20-count Red Fortune God, 167 yuan, unchanged, equivalent to Shanghai standard 172 taels and 4 mace; 16-count Fukushima, 152 yuan, unchanged, equivalent to Shanghai standard 156 taels and 9 mace; 16-count Three Horses, 152 yuan, unchanged, equivalent to Shanghai standard 156 taels and 9 mace.

Reasons for the Sharp Decline in Bombay Cotton Prices Last Week

The price decline last week was partly due to news from the American cotton market and partly due to the decline of yarn factories. Four large factories will soon cease operations, and other factories are reducing working hours. Subsequently, due to short covering, there was a slight rebound. Spot demand is not good, and exporters and manufacturers are only purchasing enough to meet immediate needs. Currently, inventories are accumulating daily. The most important issue is progress in exports. The statistics for the past week are appended below (unit: thousand bales):

Previous Week Last Week

Cumulative Receipts since September 1st 1,615 1,791

Weekend Inventory 1,147 1,229

Cumulative Exports since September 1st 873 962

Exports to Europe 317 361

Exports to China 76 76

Exports to Japan 451 496

Exports to Other Regions 29 29

Grain: Rice Market Remains Stagnant and Weak

Zhabei: Yesterday, over ten boats arrived from downriver, but sales remained sluggish. There was very little of the North Jiangsu premium japonica rice on the market. Due to flat prices, trading in mid-grade and lower-grade goods was quiet. Thin indica rice continued to arrive and sell poorly, and prices showed a strengthening trend. As sales of Yangdu indica rice were slightly more active, the market stabilized. Shops on the street in other port cities were willing to accept this rice. There was no increase or decrease. The transformation of silver dollars was stagnant, and demand was weak. The market was stagnant and soft.

South Shanghai: About ten boats arrived from downriver. Sales were stagnant and sluggish. The arrival and sales of Changshu japonica rice were both slow, and prices showed a slight weakness. However, the prices of Suzhou and Tongzhou white japonica rice rebounded slightly, but sentiment was poor, and buyers were hesitant to observe. Therefore, although supply was short, there was no intention to actively purchase. There were even fewer inquiries about South Jiangsu thin early rice, and prices fell by a dime. Yangdu indica rice trading on the street remained active, and news that Saigon foreign rice was trending firmer was also a major factor in stabilizing prices. The transformation of silver dollars was stagnant and mediocre, with small fluctuations.

Foreign Rice Continues to Rise by a Dime or So

Yesterday's foreign rice market saw little spot trading, but prices continued to improve. This was because, in addition to the rice released from previous unloading, rice arriving in port over the past few days was purchased by local buyers. Yesterday, merchants from this street and Ningbo and North Jiangsu villages in the interior all made inquiries, and the market price immediately rose by a dime or so. It was estimated that over a thousand bags of No. 1 Saigon were sold at 14.20 to 14.10 yuan, and 700 bags of No. 2 were sold at 13.80 to 13.75 yuan. Upcoming shipments are performing as well as spot goods, and prices have also risen by nearly a dime. It was estimated that 500 bags of Xiaojiao for delivery in seven days were sold at 13.26 yuan, and 3,000 bags for delivery within the month were sold at 13 yuan. Foreign firms were quite willing to sell forward contracts, but importers were very reluctant, so the market trend turned weak. It was estimated that 1,000 bags of No. 2 Saigon for February delivery were sold back at 6 taels, 2 mace, and 1 fen, and 2,000 bags of No. 1 for April delivery were sold at 6 taels, 2 mace, and 3 fen. 400 tons of Min Dang for February delivery were sold at 6 taels, 4 mace, and 5 fen, it was said.

Flour Market Weakens and Then Rebounds

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices for all months continued to trend downward. The price of Tianjin spot flour was quoted at only 3.71 yuan, which was 4 fen lower than the highest price a few days ago. Initially, seeing that the price of foreign flour had stabilized, local merchants were not very optimistic. Therefore, from the opening to the closing, selling pressure was very strong, causing the market to decline steadily. When the market opened in the afternoon, the prices for all months followed the downward trend of the morning, and the market sentiment was at its lowest since the opening of trading. The lowest price for the current month was 2 taels, 5 mace, and 9 fen, for March it was 2 taels, 5 mace, 8 fen, and 7.5 li, for April it was 2 taels, 5 mace, and 6 fen, for May it was 2 taels, 4 mace, 8 fen, and 7.5 li, for June it was 2 taels, 2 mace, and 7.5 fen, and for July it was 2 taels, 2 mace, 5 fen, and 2.5 li, a drop of 1 to 2 fen from the previous weekend. However, after the second or third round of trading, the market suddenly rebounded, as merchants from Nanjing, Wuxi, Suzhou, and other inland areas were buying both near-term and long-term contracts. As a result, the market turned stable again. Consequently, the price for the current month was up 1 fen from the previous weekend, the price for March was up 1 fen and 2.5 li, the price for April was up 7.5 li, the price for May was down 1 fen and 7.5 li, the price for June was down 7.5 li, and the price for July was down 1 fen and 2.5 li, it was said.

Interior Merchants Starting to Resell Wheat Futures

After the opening of both the morning and afternoon sessions of the wheat futures market yesterday, all months showed a sluggish trend. After the price of flour fell the previous week, interior merchants' sentiment turned and those who had previously been reluctant to sell began to consider reselling. Compared to previous years, the price of new wheat was still at a high level. Therefore, selling was active and the market fell. As a result, the price for February was not opened, the price for March was down slightly by 2 fen from the previous week's closing price, April was down by 5 fen, June was down by 2 fen, and July was down by 3 fen. The spot wheat market was quiet due to depleted inventories and slow factory demand. Dongtai wheat was sold for 5 taels, 2 mace, and 7 fen, for over 1,000 bags, it was said.

Rapeseed Sales to the East Gradually Increase

▲ Soybean Futures Firm

Yesterday, the source of rapeseed was not abundant, and the market for sales to Eastern merchants in this port was gradually increasing. Prices were similar to the previous day, with 1,066 bags of Jiujiang goods opening at 5 taels, 3 mace, and 5 fen. The soybean market suddenly turned firm, and the arrival of goods from various sources was scarce. Interior merchants' purchasing interest was strong. The market trend remained tight. Three trucks of Dalian Pingge Yuan soybeans, 1,000 bags of Hankou delayed soybeans, and 580 bags of Zha soybeans, as well as 200 bags of Jiujiang winter soybeans, opened yesterday. All prices were the same as the previous day. There were transactions in both near-term and long-term standard soybean futures, and the market trend was stable. Both buyers and sellers were gradually paying attention, it seems.

Sundries: White Hyacinth Beans Spring Market Rises 3 Taels

White hyacinth beans produced in Linghu were sold for 14 to 15 taels last autumn due to poor harvests. Since the beginning of spring, sales to Guangdong have increased again. However, inventories are scarce, and prices have risen sharply. Initial market prices sold for 17 and a half taels. There were scattered sales yesterday, and prices rose again by several qian. Therefore, market prices have already reached 18 taels. It is said that Guangdong buyers are still searching for supplies, and the trend is firm and bullish, with a continuous upward trend.

Textiles: Textile Market Extremely Stable

Local Cotton Fabric Market: There has been no major change since the red market. The downward trend in yarn and cotton prices has had no impact. The reason is that holders are unwilling to sell, and people generally expect that actual sales will improve after the Lantern Festival, with a possible upward trend. Yesterday, the fine cloth items Trumpet Child, Colored Ball, Yang Crane, and Blue Double Fish all sold for 6 taels, 6 mace, and 5 fen. Blue Chicken and Fortune God both sold for 6 taels and 3 mace. Fine twill Yang Crane remained at 6 taels, 6 mace, and 5 fen, and Blue Double Fish sold for 6 taels and 4 mace, and 5 fen. Nine-pound cloth Jubao Basin opened at 4 taels and 2 mace, and the rest were all 4 taels and 3 mace. Eleven-pound cloth Renzhong was sold for 4 taels, 8 to 9 mace. The heavy-weight cloth market was particularly sluggish because the Northern merchants had not yet started to act. Customer sales: the Jiujiang merchants purchased 100 pieces of fine cloth, and the interior merchants were also gradually becoming active.

Eastern and Western Textiles: The market was also stable. Yesterday, only the Blue Striped Satin of "Eastern Goods" showed a slightly firm trend, with more active sales. Four Scholars opened at 1 qian, 7 fen, and 2.5 li. Mei Lanfang opened at 1 qian and 7 fen, Lovely Beauty opened at 1 qian and 7 fen. Merchants from Hankou, Wuhu, Ningbo, and other places also added over a hundred pieces of Flower Brand. White Ground sold for 4 taels and 2 mace, and Huilong Pavilion Colorful sold for 4 taels and 2 mace, and 5 fen. However, the products of Lun Chang in this port and Shanghai Printing Factory also sold well in the market, with prices all around 4 taels. The fine cloth Shile Bird was in high demand on this street, with an opening price of 7 taels and 6 mace. Since the "Western Goods" rose in price, actual sales remained sluggish. Yesterday, the Changjiang merchants slightly purchased bleached cloth, with Tianxiang Jinjiu Deer at 13 taels and 1 qian, Fair Mother and Child at 10 taels and 2.5 fen, and Deji Jiude at 9 taels and 7 qian. The Fuchou merchants on this street wrote in for more than 30 pieces, it was said.

Silk and Tea: Shanghai White Filature Silk Rises Another 10 Taels

Yesterday, the market price of white filature silk in foreign firms in this port continued to rise. It was found that the inventory of dry cocoons in Shanghai warehouses was increasingly thin, the production of silk was limited, and European and American firms were actively purchasing, resulting in a shortage of supply and demand, and prices rose further. Yesterday, Lianna and others imported 50 packages of high- and mid-grade Shanghai filature silk, and the price rose by another 10 taels. Zhonghe and others imported 20 packages of white dry cocoons, and the price was also stable, it was said.

Over Two Hundred Pieces of Dry Cocoons Shipped from Wuxi to Shanghai

Last year, the spring and summer cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces reported poor harvests. Factories reduced their labor and stopped their machines due to insufficient raw materials. Over twenty factories in this port, including Xinchang, are scheduled to continue their machine operations tomorrow (12th) to reel silk, and there is a great need for cocoons. Merchants with spare cocoons are taking the opportunity to ship their stored dry cocoons from the interior to Shanghai for sale. Yesterday, the Shanghai-Wuxi passenger train also transported 240 pieces of Wuxi dry cocoons to Shanghai, which are awaiting sale in the warehouse, it was said.

Shanghai Market

Business News

Sincere Company Silk and Satin Department New Arrivals of Spring Goods: Sincere Company announced that its silk and satin department on the second floor recently received a large shipment of silk and wool fabrics, gold and silver wool fabrics, real silk velvet printed soft satin, and double-width printed silk, etc., from famous Swiss factories, no less than dozens of varieties. The organization is particularly novel, and the colors are unusually bright to meet the needs of ladies from all walks of life. They are now on display in the department, and the variety is dazzling, so customers have been very enthusiastic in recent days, etc.

Publication News

The Complete Book of Soap Manufacturing to be Published: China's soap manufacturing industry is still in its infancy, and in many cases, the methods are not good, resulting in poor products, heavy costs. Dr. Wang Tianxiang, an engineer, has worked in major European soap factories for many years and knows the progress of modern new methods. He has specially compiled this book to guide future generations. The whole book is a large volume, covering all the secrets of making all kinds of laundry soap, medicated soap, scented soap, soap powder, soap paste, etc., as well as the self-manufacture of raw materials and the collection of by-products. A volume on candle manufacturing is also appended at the end, which is also detailed and practical. The whole book is scheduled to be published at the end of March, and pre-orders will be accepted until March 10th. The pre-order price is only 2 yuan per copy, limited to 1,000 copies. Pre-orders can be placed at Delong Drug Company, located at Anji Lane, Jixiang Road, Shigaota Road, and Dasheng Advertising Company, located at Nangaoshou Lane, Haining Road.

Medical News

Dr. Zheng Yeqiao Returns to Shanghai: Dr. Zheng Yeqiao, an expert in Chinese medicine, practices medicine at Shouchun Lane, Maitehessituo Road, in this port, and has a branch clinic at Gujia Lane, Ningbo Road. Many people seek treatment from him. He returned to Haining at the end of the year to spend the New Year. Now Mr. Zheng has returned to Shanghai and is still receiving patients at his original locations, it was said.

Theater News

Paris Theater Showing "Tears of the Passionate Sea" Starting Today: The Paris Theater announced that since the showing of the war and love epic "Barking on the Battlefield," the theater has been sold out every day. As there are many famous films waiting to be shown, the theater will be replaced with the swashbuckling epic "Tears of the Passionate Sea" starting today. The film is a masterpiece by the great writer Lei Sibo Xu, co-starring the major stars Bai Li Mua Nuo and Men Kai Lai. It has extremely exciting plots and is matched with the background of snow-covered ice mountains, a grand spectacle. The whole play thoroughly breaks the concepts of racial marriage, which is especially commendable. The theater will provide tea and snacks for the gallery seats as a courtesy to the audience, it was said.

Yueming Company Releases Two New Epics: Yueming Company announced that the female bodyguard martial arts epic recently produced by the company's director, Ren Pengnian, has been released and sells well in various ports, and is well received by the audience. However, although the four-episode "Kanto Swordsman" has received letters and telegrams urging purchase from various film merchants, the shooting of the large-scale "Midnight Church" has not yet been completed due to continuous rain and snow last month. It has now been built and completed. Yesterday, the scene of the church leader Li Dahua preaching was filmed at the studio. Dahua used various illusions and showed his skills in bringing the dead back to life to bewitch the ignorant. More and more men and women blindly followed. Dahua sat majestically, his concubines standing around him, and the ceremonial guards were lined up, like the majesty of an emperor. Hundreds of believers stood under the stage. As a result, the swordsman Cha Shixiong, in order to find his cousin Zhang Yunlong, pretended to be a believer and joined forces with the two great swordsmen Zhao Yaoniang and Sun Mingfu, as well as the township regiment leader and hundreds of soldiers, to attack the church, sweep away the mechanisms, and engage in a fierce battle with the various believers. The fighting in the play has different variations in each scene and is extremely exciting and outstanding, it was said.
